							[set_specials]
								mode="append"
								[chance_to_hit]
									multiply=0.5

											[/not]

				[/delay]

			[event]
				first_time_only=no
				name="unit hits,unit misses"
				[filter_attack]
					special_id="smoke"
				[/filter_attack]
				[set_variable]
					name="weaponSpecialSmoke_side"
					value="$unit.side"
				[/set_variable]
				[set_variable]
					name="weaponSpecialSmoke_x"
					value="$second_unit.x"
				[/set_variable]
				[set_variable]
					name="weaponSpecialSmoke_y"
					value="$second_unit.y"
				[/set_variable]
				[fire_event]
					name="weaponSpecialSmoke_clear_$weaponSpecialSmoke_x|_$weaponSpecialSmoke_y"
				[/fire_event]
				[item]
					halo="halo/smoke/[0001~0015].png~SCALE(130,100)~GS()"
					name="weaponSpecialSmoke_cloud"
					x="$weaponSpecialSmoke_x"
					y="$weaponSpecialSmoke_y"
				[/item]
				[modify_unit]
					[filter]
					[/filter]
					[object]
						duration="scenario"
						id="weaponSpecialSmoke_debuff_acc_$weaponSpecialSmoke_x|_$weaponSpecialSmoke_y"
						[effect]
							apply_to="attack"
							[set_specials]
								mode="append"
								[chance_to_hit]
									multiply=0.5
									[filter_self]
										x="$weaponSpecialSmoke_x"
										y="$weaponSpecialSmoke_y"
										[filter_weapon]
											[not]
												special_id="magical"
											[/not]
										[/filter_weapon]
									[/filter_self]
								[/chance_to_hit]
							[/set_specials]
						[/effect]
					[/object]
				[/modify_unit]
				[event]
					delayed_variable_substitution=no
					first_time_only=no
					id="weaponSpecialSmoke_unitplaced_$weaponSpecialSmoke_x|_$weaponSpecialSmoke_y"
					name="unit placed"
					[modify_unit]
						[filter]
							id="$|unit.id"
						[/filter]
						[object]
							duration="scenario"
							id="weaponSpecialSmoke_debuff_acc_$weaponSpecialSmoke_x|_$weaponSpecialSmoke_y"
							[effect]

						y="$weaponSpecialSmoke_y"
